           function showfixedsizes() {
                        if($('#customsizes').css('display') == 'none') {
                                $('#customsizes').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                        }
                        if($('#moresizes').css('display') != 'none') {
                                $('#moresizes').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                        }
                    }
                    function emptyurlclass() {
                        $("#submiturl").attr("class", "");
                        return true;
                    }
                    function isNumberKey(evt) {
                        var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
                        var charInserted = String.fromCharCode(charCode);
                        var eventID = evt.target.id;
                        if (charCode &gt; 31 &amp;&amp; (charCode &lt; 48 || charCode &gt; 57)  &amp;&amp; (charCode != 46)) {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') == 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            return false;
                        } else {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 0 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            //update ajax url if everything ent well till this step
                            //smenu {dnd: 'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=OriginATTRIBU=Large=22=Size', ajaxurl:'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=OriginATTRIBU=Large=22=Size', gapush:'no'}
                            var submiturl = $("#submiturl").attr('class');
                            var val1 = $("#numbersOnly1").val();
                            var val2 = $("#numbersOnly2").val();
                            var val3 = $("#numbersOnly3").val();
                            var val4 = $("#numbersOnly4").val();

                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly1') { val1 = val1 + charInserted; }
                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly2') { val2 = val2 + charInserted; }
                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly3') { val3 = val3 + charInserted; }
                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly4') { val4 = val4 + charInserted; }

                            var measurement = $('#measurement').val();

                            if(measurement == 'cm') {
                                var vall1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1));
                                var vall2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2));
                                var vall3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3));
                                var vall4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4));
                            } else {
                                if(val1.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch1=0; }
                                if(val2.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch2=0; }
                                if(val3.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch3=0; }
                                if(val4.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch4=0; }

                                if(!inch1) { inch1=0; }
                                if(!inch2) { inch2=0; }
                                if(!inch3) { inch3=0; }
                                if(!inch4) { inch4=0; }

                                /*var vall1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1)*30.48)+inch1;
                                var vall2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2)*30.48)+inch2;
                                var vall3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3)*30.48)+inch3;
                                var vall4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4)*30.48)+inch4;*/
                                var vall1 = val1;
                                var vall2 = val2;
                                var vall3 = val3;
                                var vall4 = val4;
                            }

                            var valall = vall1+"-"+vall2+"x"+vall3+"-"+vall4+" fts";
                            var adsignadsign = "";
                            var docurl = document.URL;
                            if(docurl.indexOf("ATTRIBU=") &gt; -1) {
                                adsignadsign = "@@";
                            }
                            var newclass = "smenu {dnd: 'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=Origin"+adsignadsign+"ATTRIBU="+valall+"=22=Size', ajaxurl:'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=Origin"+adsignadsign+"ATTRIBU="+valall+"=22=Size', gapush:'no'}";
                            if((parseFloat(val1) &gt; parseFloat(val2))) {
                               newclass = "";
                            }
                            if((parseFloat(val3) &gt; parseFloat(val4))) {
                               newclass = "";
                            }
                            if(val1=='From') {
                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            if(val2=='To') {
                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            if(val3=='From') {
                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            if(val4=='To') {
                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            if((!vall1) || (!vall2) || (!vall3) || (!vall4) || (inchh1&gt;11) || (inchh2&gt;11) || (inchh3&gt;11) || (inchh4&gt;11)) {
                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            $("#submiturl").attr("class", newclass);
                            return true;
                        }
                    }
                    function ValidateCustomWidthForm() {
                        var charValue1 = $('#numbersOnly1').val();
                        var charValue2 = $('#numbersOnly2').val();
                        var charValue3 = $('#numbersOnly3').val();
                        var charValue4 = $('#numbersOnly4').val();
                        var inchh1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue1.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue2.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue3.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue4.split('.')[1]));


                        if((charValue1 != 'From') &amp;&amp; (charValue3 != 'From') &amp;&amp; (charValue2 != 'To') &amp;&amp; (charValue4 != 'To')) {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if(parseFloat(charValue1) &gt; parseFloat(charValue2)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }
                            if(parseFloat(charValue3) &gt; parseFloat(charValue4)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }
                            if(!parseInt(charValue1) || !parseInt(charValue2) || !parseInt(charValue3) || !parseInt(charValue4)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }
                            if((inchh1 &gt; 11) || (inchh2 &gt; 11) || (inchh3 &gt; 11) || (inchh4 &gt; 11)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr5').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr5').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr5').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr5').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }


                            return true;													
                        } else {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') == 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            return false;
                        }
                        }

           function showfixedsizes() {
                        if($('#customsizes').css('display') == 'none') {
                                $('#customsizes').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                        }
                        if($('#moresizes').css('display') != 'none') {
                                $('#moresizes').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                        }
                    }
                    function emptyurlclass() {
                        $("#submiturl").attr("class", "");
                        return true;
                    }
                    function isNumberKey(evt) {
                        var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
                        var charInserted = String.fromCharCode(charCode);
                        var eventID = evt.target.id;
                        if (charCode &gt; 31 &amp;&amp; (charCode &lt; 48 || charCode &gt; 57)  &amp;&amp; (charCode != 46)) {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') == 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            return false;
                        } else {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 0 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            //update ajax url if everything ent well till this step
                            //smenu {dnd: 'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=OriginATTRIBU=Large=22=Size', ajaxurl:'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=OriginATTRIBU=Large=22=Size', gapush:'no'}
                            var submiturl = $("#submiturl").attr('class');
                            var val1 = $("#numbersOnly1").val();
                            var val2 = $("#numbersOnly2").val();
                            var val3 = $("#numbersOnly3").val();
                            var val4 = $("#numbersOnly4").val();

                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly1') { val1 = val1 + charInserted; }
                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly2') { val2 = val2 + charInserted; }
                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly3') { val3 = val3 + charInserted; }
                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly4') { val4 = val4 + charInserted; }

                            var measurement = $('#measurement').val();

                            if(measurement == 'cm') {
                                var vall1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1));
                                var vall2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2));
                                var vall3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3));
                                var vall4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4));
                            } else {
                                if(val1.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch1=0; }
                                if(val2.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch2=0; }
                                if(val3.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch3=0; }
                                if(val4.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch4=0; }

                                if(!inch1) { inch1=0; }
                                if(!inch2) { inch2=0; }
                                if(!inch3) { inch3=0; }
                                if(!inch4) { inch4=0; }

                                /*var vall1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1)*30.48)+inch1;
                                var vall2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2)*30.48)+inch2;
                                var vall3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3)*30.48)+inch3;
                                var vall4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4)*30.48)+inch4;*/
                                var vall1 = val1;
                                var vall2 = val2;
                                var vall3 = val3;
                                var vall4 = val4;
                            }

                            var valall = vall1+"-"+vall2+"x"+vall3+"-"+vall4+" fts";
                            var adsignadsign = "";
                            var docurl = document.URL;
                            if(docurl.indexOf("ATTRIBU=") &gt; -1) {
                                adsignadsign = "@@";
                            }

                    function ValidateCustomWidthForm() {

                    function isNumberKey(evt) {
                        var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
                        var charInserted = String.fromCharCode(charCode);
                        var eventID = evt.target.id;
                        if (charCode &gt; 31 &amp;&amp; (charCode &lt; 48 || charCode &gt; 57)  &amp;&amp; (charCode != 46)) {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {

                            }

                                if(val2.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {

                    function ValidateCustomWidthForm() {
                        var charValue1 = $('#numbersOnly1').val();
                        var charValue2 = $('#numbersOnly2').val();
                        var charValue3 = $('#numbersOnly3').val();
                        var charValue4 = $('#numbersOnly4').val();
                        var inchh1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue1.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue2.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue3.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue4.split('.')[1]));


                        if((charValue1 != 'From') &amp;&amp; (charValue3 != 'From') &amp;&amp; (charValue2 != 'To') &amp;&amp; (charValue4 != 'To')) {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if(parseFloat(charValue1) &gt; parseFloat(charValue2)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }

                                }

                                }
                            }


                            return true;													
                        } else {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') == 'none') {

           function showfixedsizes() {
                        if($('#customsizes').css('display') == 'none') {
                                $('#customsizes').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });

                    function emptyurlclass() {

                        return true;
                    }
                    function isNumberKey(evt) {
                        var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
                        var charInserted = String.fromCharCode(charCode);
                        var eventID = evt.target.id;
                        if (charCode &gt; 31 &amp;&amp; (charCode &lt; 48 || charCode &gt; 57)  &amp;&amp; (charCode != 46)) {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') == 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            return false;
                        } else {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 0 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            //update ajax url if everything ent well till this step
                            //smenu {dnd: 'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=OriginATTRIBU=Large=22=Size', ajaxurl:'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=OriginATTRIBU=Large=22=Size', gapush:'no'}
                            var submiturl = $("#submiturl").attr('class');
                            var val1 = $("#numbersOnly1").val();
                            var val2 = $("#numbersOnly2").val();
                            var val3 = $("#numbersOnly3").val();
                            var val4 = $("#numbersOnly4").val();

                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly1') { val1 = val1 + charInserted; }
                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly2') { val2 = val2 + charInserted; }
                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly3') { val3 = val3 + charInserted; }
                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly4') { val4 = val4 + charInserted; }

                            var measurement = $('#measurement').val();

                            if(measurement == 'cm') {
                                var vall1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1));
                                var vall2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2));
                                var vall3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3));
                                var vall4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4));
                            } else {
                                if(val1.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch1=0; }
                                if(val2.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch2=0; }
                                if(val3.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch3=0; }
                                if(val4.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch4=0; }

                                if(!inch1) { inch1=0; }
                                if(!inch2) { inch2=0; }
                                if(!inch3) { inch3=0; }
                                if(!inch4) { inch4=0; }

                                /*var vall1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1)*30.48)+inch1;
                                var vall2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2)*30.48)+inch2;
                                var vall3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3)*30.48)+inch3;
                                var vall4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4)*30.48)+inch4;*/
                                var vall1 = val1;
                                var vall2 = val2;
                                var vall3 = val3;
                                var vall4 = val4;
                            }

                            var valall = vall1+"-"+vall2+"x"+vall3+"-"+vall4+" fts";
                            var adsignadsign = "";
                            var docurl = document.URL;
                            if(docurl.indexOf("ATTRIBU=") &gt; -1) {
                                adsignadsign = "@@";
                            }
                            var newclass = "smenu {dnd: 'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=Origin"+adsignadsign+"ATTRIBU="+valall+"=22=Size', ajaxurl:'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=Origin"+adsignadsign+"ATTRIBU="+valall+"=22=Size', gapush:'no'}";
                            if((parseFloat(val1) &gt; parseFloat(val2))) {
                               newclass = "";
                            }
                            if((parseFloat(val3) &gt; parseFloat(val4))) {
                               newclass = "";
                            }
                            if(val1=='From') {
                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            if(val2=='To') {
                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            if(val3=='From') {
                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            if(val4=='To') {
                                newclass = "";
                            }

                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            $("#submiturl").attr("class", newclass);
                            return true;
                        }
                    }
                    function ValidateCustomWidthForm() {
                        var charValue1 = $('#numbersOnly1').val();
                        var charValue2 = $('#numbersOnly2').val();
                        var charValue3 = $('#numbersOnly3').val();
                        var charValue4 = $('#numbersOnly4').val();
                        var inchh1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue1.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue2.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue3.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue4.split('.')[1]));


                        if((charValue1 != 'From') &amp;&amp; (charValue3 != 'From') &amp;&amp; (charValue2 != 'To') &amp;&amp; (charValue4 != 'To')) {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if(parseFloat(charValue1) &gt; parseFloat(charValue2)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }
                            if(parseFloat(charValue3) &gt; parseFloat(charValue4)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }
                            if(!parseInt(charValue1) || !parseInt(charValue2) || !parseInt(charValue3) || !parseInt(charValue4)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }
                            if((inchh1 &gt; 11) || (inchh2 &gt; 11) || (inchh3 &gt; 11) || (inchh4 &gt; 11)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr5').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr5').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr5').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr5').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }


                            return true;													
                        } else {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') == 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            return false;
                        }
                        }

                    function isNumberKey(evt) {
                        var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
                        var charInserted = String.fromCharCode(charCode);
                        var eventID = evt.target.id;
                        if (charCode &gt; 31 &amp;&amp; (charCode &lt; 48 || charCode &gt; 57)  &amp;&amp; (charCode != 46)) {

                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });

                    function isNumberKey(evt) {
                        var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
                        var charInserted = String.fromCharCode(charCode);
                        var eventID = evt.target.id;
                        if (charCode &gt; 31 &amp;&amp; (charCode &lt; 48 || charCode &gt; 57)  &amp;&amp; (charCode != 46)) {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') == 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            return false;
                        } else {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 0 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            //update ajax url if everything ent well till this step
                            //smenu {dnd: 'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=OriginATTRIBU=Large=22=Size', ajaxurl:'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=OriginATTRIBU=Large=22=Size', gapush:'no'}
                            var submiturl = $("#submiturl").attr('class');
                            var val1 = $("#numbersOnly1").val();
                            var val2 = $("#numbersOnly2").val();
                            var val3 = $("#numbersOnly3").val();
                            var val4 = $("#numbersOnly4").val();

                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly1') { val1 = val1 + charInserted; }
                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly2') { val2 = val2 + charInserted; }
                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly3') { val3 = val3 + charInserted; }
                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly4') { val4 = val4 + charInserted; }

                            var measurement = $('#measurement').val();

                            if(measurement == 'cm') {
                                var vall1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1));
                                var vall2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2));
                                var vall3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3));
                                var vall4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4));
                            } else {
                                if(val1.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch1=0; }
                                if(val2.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch2=0; }
                                if(val3.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch3=0; }
                                if(val4.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch4=0; }

                                if(!inch1) { inch1=0; }
                                if(!inch2) { inch2=0; }
                                if(!inch3) { inch3=0; }
                                if(!inch4) { inch4=0; }

                                /*var vall1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1)*30.48)+inch1;
                                var vall2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2)*30.48)+inch2;
                                var vall3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3)*30.48)+inch3;
                                var vall4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4)*30.48)+inch4;*/

                                var vall2 = val2;
                                var vall3 = val3;
                                var vall4 = val4;
                            }

                            var valall = vall1+"-"+vall2+"x"+vall3+"-"+vall4+" fts";
                            var adsignadsign = "";
                            var docurl = document.URL;
                            if(docurl.indexOf("ATTRIBU=") &gt; -1) {
                                adsignadsign = "@@";
                            }
                            var newclass = "smenu {dnd: 'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=Origin"+adsignadsign+"ATTRIBU="+valall+"=22=Size', ajaxurl:'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=Origin"+adsignadsign+"ATTRIBU="+valall+"=22=Size', gapush:'no'}";
                            if((parseFloat(val1) &gt; parseFloat(val2))) {
                               newclass = "";
                            }
                            if((parseFloat(val3) &gt; parseFloat(val4))) {
                               newclass = "";
                            }
                            if(val1=='From') {
                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            if(val2=='To') {
                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            if(val3=='From') {
                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            if(val4=='To') {
                                newclass = "";
                            }

                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            $("#submiturl").attr("class", newclass);
                            return true;
                        }

                    function ValidateCustomWidthForm() {
                        var charValue1 = $('#numbersOnly1').val();
                        var charValue2 = $('#numbersOnly2').val();
                        var charValue3 = $('#numbersOnly3').val();
                        var charValue4 = $('#numbersOnly4').val();
                        var inchh1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue1.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue2.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue3.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue4.split('.')[1]));


                        if((charValue1 != 'From') &amp;&amp; (charValue3 != 'From') &amp;&amp; (charValue2 != 'To') &amp;&amp; (charValue4 != 'To')) {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if(parseFloat(charValue1) &gt; parseFloat(charValue2)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }
                            if(parseFloat(charValue3) &gt; parseFloat(charValue4)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }
                            if(!parseInt(charValue1) || !parseInt(charValue2) || !parseInt(charValue3) || !parseInt(charValue4)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }
                            if((inchh1 &gt; 11) || (inchh2 &gt; 11) || (inchh3 &gt; 11) || (inchh4 &gt; 11)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr5').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr5').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr5').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr5').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }


                            return true;													
                        } else {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') == 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {

                    function isNumberKey(evt) {
                        var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
                        var charInserted = String.fromCharCode(charCode);
                        var eventID = evt.target.id;
                        if (charCode &gt; 31 &amp;&amp; (charCode &lt; 48 || charCode &gt; 57)  &amp;&amp; (charCode != 46)) {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }

                            }
                            return false;

                                if(val2.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {

                                } else { inch4=0; }

                    function ValidateCustomWidthForm() {
                        var charValue1 = $('#numbersOnly1').val();
                        var charValue2 = $('#numbersOnly2').val();
                        var charValue3 = $('#numbersOnly3').val();
                        var charValue4 = $('#numbersOnly4').val();
                        var inchh1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue1.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue2.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue3.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue4.split('.')[1]));


                        if((charValue1 != 'From') &amp;&amp; (charValue3 != 'From') &amp;&amp; (charValue2 != 'To') &amp;&amp; (charValue4 != 'To')) {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if(parseFloat(charValue1) &gt; parseFloat(charValue2)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }
                            if(parseFloat(charValue3) &gt; parseFloat(charValue4)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {

                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') == 'none') {

                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }
                            if(!parseInt(charValue1) || !parseInt(charValue2) || !parseInt(charValue3) || !parseInt(charValue4)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }

                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }
                            if((inchh1 &gt; 11) || (inchh2 &gt; 11) || (inchh3 &gt; 11) || (inchh4 &gt; 11)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }

                    function isNumberKey(evt) {

                    function ValidateCustomWidthForm() {
                        var charValue1 = $('#numbersOnly1').val();
                        var charValue2 = $('#numbersOnly2').val();
                        var charValue3 = $('#numbersOnly3').val();
                        var charValue4 = $('#numbersOnly4').val();
                        var inchh1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue1.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue2.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue3.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue4.split('.')[1]));


                        if((charValue1 != 'From') &amp;&amp; (charValue3 != 'From') &amp;&amp; (charValue2 != 'To') &amp;&amp; (charValue4 != 'To')) {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if(parseFloat(charValue1) &gt; parseFloat(charValue2)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {

                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });

           function showfixedsizes() {
                        if($('#customsizes').css('display') == 'none') {
                                $('#customsizes').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                        }
                        if($('#moresizes').css('display') != 'none') {

                    function emptyurlclass() {

                        return true;

                    function isNumberKey(evt) {
                        var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
                        var charInserted = String.fromCharCode(charCode);
                        var eventID = evt.target.id;
                        if (charCode &gt; 31 &amp;&amp; (charCode &lt; 48 || charCode &gt; 57)  &amp;&amp; (charCode != 46)) {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') == 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            return false;
                        } else {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 0 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            //update ajax url if everything ent well till this step
                            //smenu {dnd: 'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=OriginATTRIBU=Large=22=Size', ajaxurl:'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=OriginATTRIBU=Large=22=Size', gapush:'no'}
                            var submiturl = $("#submiturl").attr('class');
                            var val1 = $("#numbersOnly1").val();
                            var val2 = $("#numbersOnly2").val();
                            var val3 = $("#numbersOnly3").val();
                            var val4 = $("#numbersOnly4").val();

                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly1') { val1 = val1 + charInserted; }
                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly2') { val2 = val2 + charInserted; }
                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly3') { val3 = val3 + charInserted; }
                            if(eventID == 'numbersOnly4') { val4 = val4 + charInserted; }

                            var measurement = $('#measurement').val();

                            if(measurement == 'cm') {
                                var vall1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1));
                                var vall2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2));
                                var vall3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3));
                                var vall4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4));
                            } else {
                                if(val1.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch1=0; }
                                if(val2.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch2=0; }
                                if(val3.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch3=0; }
                                if(val4.indexOf(".") &gt; -1) {
                                    var inchh4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4.split('.')[1]));
                                    var inch4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4.split('.')[1])*2.54);
                                } else { inch4=0; }

                                if(!inch1) { inch1=0; }
                                if(!inch2) { inch2=0; }
                                if(!inch3) { inch3=0; }
                                if(!inch4) { inch4=0; }

                                /*var vall1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val1)*30.48)+inch1;
                                var vall2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val2)*30.48)+inch2;
                                var vall3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val3)*30.48)+inch3;
                                var vall4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(val4)*30.48)+inch4;*/
                                var vall1 = val1;
                                var vall2 = val2;
                                var vall3 = val3;
                                var vall4 = val4;
                            }

                            var valall = vall1+"-"+vall2+"x"+vall3+"-"+vall4+" fts";
                            var adsignadsign = "";
                            var docurl = document.URL;
                            if(docurl.indexOf("ATTRIBU=") &gt; -1) {
                                adsignadsign = "@@";
                            }
                            var newclass = "smenu {dnd: 'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=Origin"+adsignadsign+"ATTRIBU="+valall+"=22=Size', ajaxurl:'https://www.rugman.com/index.php?route=product/asearch&amp;path=6&amp;filter=ATTRIBU=Persian=2=Origin"+adsignadsign+"ATTRIBU="+valall+"=22=Size', gapush:'no'}";
                            if((parseFloat(val1) &gt; parseFloat(val2))) {
                               newclass = "";
                            }
                            if((parseFloat(val3) &gt; parseFloat(val4))) {
                               newclass = "";
                            }
                            if(val1=='From') {
                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            if(val2=='To') {
                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            if(val3=='From') {
                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            if(val4=='To') {
                                newclass = "";
                            }

                                newclass = "";
                            }
                            $("#submiturl").attr("class", newclass);
                            return true;
                        }

                    function ValidateCustomWidthForm() {
                        var charValue1 = $('#numbersOnly1').val();
                        var charValue2 = $('#numbersOnly2').val();
                        var charValue3 = $('#numbersOnly3').val();
                        var charValue4 = $('#numbersOnly4').val();
                        var inchh1 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue1.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh2 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue2.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh3 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue3.split('.')[1]));
                        var inchh4 = Math.ceil(parseInt(charValue4.split('.')[1]));


                        if((charValue1 != 'From') &amp;&amp; (charValue3 != 'From') &amp;&amp; (charValue2 != 'To') &amp;&amp; (charValue4 != 'To')) {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if(parseFloat(charValue1) &gt; parseFloat(charValue2)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }
                            if(parseFloat(charValue3) &gt; parseFloat(charValue4)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }
                            if(!parseInt(charValue1) || !parseInt(charValue2) || !parseInt(charValue3) || !parseInt(charValue4)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }
                            if((inchh1 &gt; 11) || (inchh2 &gt; 11) || (inchh3 &gt; 11) || (inchh4 &gt; 11)) {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr5').css('display') == 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr5').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                if($('.numbersOnlyErr5').css('display') != 'none') {
                                        $('.numbersOnlyErr5').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                                }
                            }


                            return true;													
                        } else {
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr4').css('display') == 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr4').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr2').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr2').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            if($('.numbersOnlyErr3').css('display') != 'none') {
                                    $('.numbersOnlyErr3').animate({ 'height': 'toggle' }, { duration: 400 });
                            }
                            return false;
                        }
                        }
