    <script type="text/javascript">
     //OpenCart 1.5.6.4. &amp; Rugman.Com Diff START
    // deactive screen &amp; show loding image when ajax search is working
    function openModal() {
        document.getElementById('modal').style.display = 'block';
        document.getElementById('loader').style.display = 'block';
        if($('.cat_filter').css('cat_filter') != 'none') {
                $('.cat_filter').hide();
        }
        //document.getElementById('fade').style.display = 'block';
    }
    // active screen
    function closeModal() {
        document.getElementById('modal').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('loader').style.display = 'none';
        //document.getElementById('fade').style.display = 'none';
    }
    //OpenCart 1.5.6.4. &amp; Rugman.Com Diff END
    
    
    var ajaxManager = $.manageAjax.create('cacheQueue', {queue: true, cacheResponse: true});
    function Ajaxmenu(filter) {
        //OpenCart 1.5.6.4. &amp; Rugman.Com Diff START
        openModal();
        //OpenCart 1.5.6.4. &amp; Rugman.Com Diff END
        ajaxManager.add({
            success: showResponseMenu, // post-submit callback 
            url: 'index.php?route=module/supercategorymenuadvanced/MenuAjax',
            data: filter,
            type: "GET",
            cache: true
        });
        ajaxManager.add({
            success: showResponsedatos, // post-submit callback 
            url: 'index.php?route=product/asearch/asearchAjax',
            data: filter,
            type: "GET",
            cache: true
        });
    }
    ;
    var ajaxManager2 = $.manageAjax.create('cacheQueue', {queue: true, cacheResponse: true});
    function Ajaxmenup(filter) {
        ajaxManager2.add({
            success: showResponsedatos, // post-submit callback 
            url: 'index.php?route=product/asearch/asearchAjax',
            data: filter,
            type: "GET",
            cache: true
        });
    }
    ;
    function showResponseMenu(responseText, statusText, xhr) {
        $('#menuscm').fadeOut('slow', function() {
            $('#menuscm').fadeOut('slow');
                    $("#menuscm").replaceWith(responseText).fadeIn( 2000 );
        });
    }
    function showResponsedatos(responseText, statusText, xhr) {
      //Charkhchi=&gt;  $('.cat_top').fadeOut('slow');
        $('#content').fadeOut('slow', function() {
            $('#content').fadeOut('slow');
                    $("#content").replaceWith(responseText).fadeIn( 2000 );
        });
        $('body,html').animate({scrollTop: 150}, 800); 
        
        //OpenCart 1.5.6.4. &amp; Rugman.Com Diff START
        closeModal();
        //OpenCart 1.5.6.4. &amp; Rugman.Com Diff END
    }

    $(document).delegate("select.smenu", "change", function() {
        var jThis = $("option:selected", this), dnd, gapush, ajax_url;
        dnd = jThis.metadata().dnd;
        gapush = jThis.metadata().gapush;
        ajax_url = jThis.metadata().ajaxurl;
        if (gapush != "no"){
        var gas_val = gapush.split('@@@@@')
                _gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'SCM', gas_val[0], gas_val[1]])
        }
                        if (history.pushState) {
        History.pushState(null, ajax_url, dnd);
        } else{
        Ajaxmenu(ajax_url);
        }
                        return false;
    });
    $(document).delegate("a.smenu", "click", function() {
        var jThis = $(this), dnd, gapush, ajax_url;
        dnd = jThis.metadata().dnd;
        gapush = jThis.metadata().gapush;
        ajax_url = jThis.metadata().ajaxurl;
        if (gapush != "no"){
        var gas_val = gapush.split('@@@@@')
                _gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'SCM', gas_val[0], gas_val[1]])
        }
                        if (history.pushState) {
        History.pushState(null, ajax_url, dnd);
        } else{
        Ajaxmenu(ajax_url);
        }
                        return false;
    });
    </script>

    <h1 style="margin-bottom: 5px;">
     Persian Hand Knotted Area Rugs
    </h1>
    <div class="category-info">
     <p>
      <span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: normal;">
       Persian Area Rugs and Carpets are referred to any rug that is hand weaved in Persia. Persian rugs are world famous for their exceptional quality, incredible designs and patterns and lively colors. Persian rugs are also referred to as " State of art" which shows the superiority of this class of rug compared to the other categories of rugs that come from other regions of the world.
      </span>

&lt;script type="text/javascript"&gt;&lt;!--
function display(view) {
      if (view == 'list') {
              $('.product-grid').attr('class', 'product-list');
              
              $('.product-list &gt; div').each(function(index, element) {
                      html  = '&lt;div class="right"&gt;';
                      html += '  &lt;div class="cart"&gt;' + $(element).find('.cart').html() + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                      html += '  &lt;div class="wishlist"&gt;' + $(element).find('.wishlist').html() + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                      html += '  &lt;div class="compare"&gt;' + $(element).find('.compare').html() + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                      html += '&lt;/div&gt;';			
                      
                      html += '&lt;div class="left"&gt;';
                      
                      var image = $(element).find('.image').html();
                      
                      if (image != null) { 
                              html += '&lt;div class="image"&gt;' + image + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                      }
                      
                      var price = $(element).find('.price').html();
                      
                      if (price != null) {
                              html += '&lt;div class="price"&gt;' + price  + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                      }
                                      
                      html += '  &lt;div class="name"&gt;' + $(element).find('.name').html() + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                      html += '  &lt;div class="description"&gt;' + $(element).find('.description').html() + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                      
                      var rating = $(element).find('.rating').html();
                      
                      if (rating != null) {
                              html += '&lt;div class="rating"&gt;' + rating + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                      }
                              
                      html += '&lt;/div&gt;';
                                              
                      $(element).html(html);
              });		
              
              $('.display').html('&lt;b&gt;Display:&lt;/b&gt; List &lt;b&gt;/&lt;/b&gt; &lt;a onclick="display(\'grid\');"&gt;Grid&lt;/a&gt;');
              
              $.totalStorage('display', 'list'); 

      } else {
              $('.product-list').attr('class', 'product-grid');
              
              $('.product-grid &gt; div').each(function(index, element) {
                      html = '';
                      
                      var image = $(element).find('.image').html();
                      
                      if (image != null) {
                              html += '&lt;div class="image"&gt;' + image + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                      }
                      
                      html += '&lt;div class="name"&gt;' + $(element).find('.name').html() + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                      html += '&lt;div class="description"&gt;' + $(element).find('.description').html() + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                      
                      var price = $(element).find('.price').html();
                      
                      if (price != null) {
                              html += '&lt;div class="price"&gt;' + price  + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                      }
                      
                      var rating = $(element).find('.rating').html();
                      
                      if (rating != null) {
                              html += '&lt;div class="rating"&gt;' + rating + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                      }
                                              
                      html += '&lt;div class="cart"&gt;' + $(element).find('.cart').html() + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                      html += '&lt;div class="wishlist"&gt;' + $(element).find('.wishlist').html() + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                      html += '&lt;div class="compare"&gt;' + $(element).find('.compare').html() + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                      
                      $(element).html(html);
              });	
                                      
              $('.display').html('&lt;b&gt;Display:&lt;/b&gt; &lt;a onclick="display(\'list\');"&gt;List&lt;/a&gt; &lt;b&gt;/&lt;/b&gt; Grid');
              
              $.totalStorage('display', 'grid');

      }
}

view = $.totalStorage('display');

if (view) {
      display(view);
} else {
      display('list');
}
-->
   <script type="text/javascript">
    $("div.pagination div.links a").click(function(event){
    event.preventDefault();
            var hreflink = $(this).attr("href");
            if (hreflink.indexOf("product/asearch") != - 1){//don't have seo
            var someVar = hreflink.replace(/http(.*?)&amp;/i, "");
    } else{//have seo
    var someVar = hreflink.replace(/http(.*?)\?/i, "") + "&amp;path=0";
    }
                // History.pushState(null, ajax_url, dnd);

            Ajaxmenup(someVar);
    //}

                return false;
    });
